 navjot singh siddhuvija ke saath, vah wagha border to paar kar sakate hai lekin ek bhartiya rajya vidhayika ke nirvaachit pratinidhi ke rup main unhen raajnneetik manjuuri kii aavashyaktaa hogi
 Former Punjab minister and Congress leader Navjot Singh Sidhu on Saturday accepted Foreign Minister S
K
 jaishankar se kartarpur galiyare ke udghaatan samaaroh main shaamil hone ke liye sarkari manjuuri maangi he
 The ceremony will be held three days before the 550th birth anniversary of Guru Nanak Dev, the founder of Sikhism
 pakistan kii imran khan sarkaar dwaara 9 november ko kartarpur galiyare (coridor) ke udghaatan main bhaag lene ke liye siddhu ko aamantrit kiya gaya
 Cricketer-turned-politician Sidhu has accepted this invitation from Pakistan
 pehle raajnneetik manjuuri jaruribharat sarkaar ne pehle hi saaf kar rakhaa he ki pakistan sarkaar dwaara aamantrit kiye gaye sabhi logon ko pehle raajnneetik manjuuri leni hogi
 On receiving the invitation on this basis, Navjot Singh Sidhu on Saturday sought permission from Punjab Chief Minister Amarinder Singh and Foreign Minister s Jaishankar to participate in the event
 paak pradhanmantri imran khan ke nirdesh par sattarudh pakistan taharik-e-insaaf (pitiai) ke seenetter faisal javed ne navjot singh siddhu se sampark kiya or is saptaah kii shuruyaat main unhen is samaaroh ke liye aamantrit kiya
 Sidhu said that Sikh communities from all over the world are eager to have a glimpse of the holy temple associated with their spiritual guru Nanak Dev
 pichley saal agast main navjot singh siddhu ne imran khan ke shapath grahan samaaroh main bhi shirkat kii thi, jisaki bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ne kaaphi aalochana kii thi
 P
 bengal ke vishwa bharti parisar sthit ek skool ke chatravaas main bistar geela karne par kathith rup se apana peshaab pine kii sajaa milane se aahat 10 varshiya chaatra ko sadame se ubaarana mushkil ho rahaa he
 The student's father said this on Tuesday
 chaatra ke pita manoj mistre ne kaha, "vah abhi tak sadame se nahin ubar pai he
 She is not eating properly
 uske saath jo kuch hua, uske baad se uski manodasha saamaanya nahin ho paa rahi he
 Doctors have advised us to keep him happy and help him forget the incident
 " The student does not want to return to the school fearing that the incident may repeat
 patha bhawan skool kii kaksha paanch kii chaatra ne kaha, "main skool ke chatravaas main lautnaa nahin chaahati
 i want to study in another school
 ve mujhe phir vaisaa hi karne ke liye kah sakate hai
 " chaatra ne kaha ki mata-pita ne uskaa anurodh sweekaar kar liya he
 At the same time, Mistry said, "he is not ready to go to school after the incident
 ham kya kar sakate hai? yahi sambhav he ki ham uskaa daakhila duusare skool main karvaa den
 " usne kaha, "10 saal kii bacchee hokar jab mujhe aisi juthi baton main vishwaas nahin he tab warden in chizon main vishwaas kaise kar sakati hai?" Vishwa Bharati University officials claim that the warden Uma Poddar asked the student to lick the urine because she believes that doing so will cure bed-wetting
 is mudde par chautarafa aalochana jhelane ke baad adhikariyon ne chaatra ke mata-pita se anurodh kiya he ki ve use ghar se pratidin skool bhejein
 Poonam Mistry, the girl's mother, said, "today we got a call from the university asking that we send our daughter back to school again and not send her to the hostel and send her to school every day
 " Meanwhile, a case was registered under Section 23 of the Juvenile Justice Act after police were pulled over by the court for being soft on the warden
 is adhinium main bachche ke saath krurta se pesh aane par adhiktam chah maheene kii kaid yaa jurmaana yaa donon kaa praavdhaan he
 Superintendent of Police (birbhum) Hrishikesh Meena said, "following the court order, we have registered a case against the warden under Section 23 of the Child Justice Act
 " The incident with the student has been widely criticized and the matter has reached the Prime Minister's Office (PMO)
 rashtriya bal adhikaar sangrakshan ayog ne is maamle par vishvavidhyalay or rajya sarkaar se vistrut report maangi he
 It is reported that the Governor of West Bengal M
 ke
 Narayanan has also sought a report from the university
 purv loksabhaa adhyaksh somnath chatarji ne is ghatana ko amanviya or sharmnaak bataaya
 He said, "people send their child to the hostel in the hope that they will be better taken care of there but after this incident they cannot think so
 " According to a police complaint, the incident took place on Saturday evening when Uma Poddar, the warden of the Qarabi hostel, found the student guilty of bedwetting during surprise inspections
 aarope he ki poddar ne sajaa ke taur par chaatra ko peshaab chaatane ko kaha
 The girl is said to have told this to her mother, after which her guardian and several others rushed into the hostel premises and misbehaved with the warden
 tippaniyan After the incident, the university formed a four-member committee headed by Aruna Mukherjee, former chairperson of the Student Welfare Faculty, to investigate the matter
 report par karrwai karte hue vishvavidhyalay ne poddar ko warden ke pad se kaary-mukt kar diya he
 The student's father Manoj Mistry said, "she has not recovered from the shock yet
 vah thik se khaanaa nahin kha rahi he
 Since what happened to him, his mood has not returned to normal
 chikitsakon ne hamen use khush rakhane or ghatana ko bhulane main uski madad karne kii salaah di he
 " ghatana dohraane kii ashanka se chaatra us skool main lautnaa nahin chaahati
 a Class v student of Patha Bhavan School said, "I don't want to return to the school hostel
 main duusare skool main padhanaa chaahati hum
 They can then ask me to do the same
 " The student said that the parents have accepted her request
 vahiin, mistre ne kaha, "ghatana ke baad vah skool jane ke liye raji nahin he
 what can we do? It is possible that we get him enrolled in another school
 " He said, "how can the warden believe in these things when i am not a believer in such false things as a 10-year-old girl?" vishwa bharti vishvavidhyalay ke adhikariyon kaa daawa he ki warden uma poddar ne chaatra se isliye peshaab chaatane ke liye kaha, kyonki vah maanati hai ki aisa karne se bistar geela karne kii beemaari thik ho jaaegi
 After facing all-round criticism on this issue, the authorities have requested the parents of the student to send her to school daily from home
 chaatra kii maa punam mistre ne kaha, "aaj hamaare paas vishvavidhyalay se ek phone aayaa jisamen kaha gaya ki ham apni beti ko phir se skool bhejein or chatravaas main na rakhkar ghar se pratidin skool bhejein
 " is bich, warden ke prati narmi baratane par adaalat dwaara police kii khinchaai kiye jane ke baad bal nyaay adhinium kii dhara 23 ke tahat ek maamla darj kiya gaya
 The Act provides for imprisonment for a maximum of six months or fine or both for cruelty to a child
 police adheekshak (birbhum) rishikesh meena ne kaha, "adaalat ke aadesh kaa paalan karte hue hamane warden ke khilaaf bal nyaay adhinium kii dhara 23 ke tahat maamla darj kar liya he
 " chaatra ke saath hui ghatana kii chautarafa aalochana hui he or baat pradhanmantri karyaalay (piemo) tak pahunch gai he
 The National Commission for Protection of Child Rights has sought a detailed report from the university and the state government on the matter
 bataaya gaya he ki pashchim bengal ke rajyapal em
 K
 narayanan ne bhi vishvavidhyalay se ek report maangi he
 Former Lok Sabha Speaker Somnath Chatterjee described the incident as inhuman and shameful
 unhone kaha, "log apane bachche ko is ummid se chatravaas main bhejte hai ki vahaan uskaa behatar khyaal rakhaa jayega lekin is ghatana ke baad ve aisa nahin soch sakate
 " police main kii gai shikaayat ke mutabik, yah ghatana shanivaar shaam kii he, jab karabi chatravaas kii warden uma poddar ne auchak nirikshan ke dauraan chaatra ko bistar geela karne kaa doshi paaya
 It is alleged that Poddar asked the student to lick the urine as a punishment
 bataaya jaataa he ki bacchee ne yah baat apni maa ko bataai, jiske baad uske abhibhavak tathaa kai anya logon ne chatravaas parisar main pahunchakar warden ke saath badasluki kii
 The comments ghatana ke baad vishvavidhyalay ne maamle kii jaanch ke liye chaatr kalyaan sankaay kii purv adhyaksh aruna mukherjee kii adhyakshata main chaar sadasyeey samiti kaa gathan kiya

 bharat ke prayek rajya or centreshasit pradesh kaa apana alag police bal he
